**You need to turn on Javascript to see the content of this entry correctly.**<br/>
</noscript>

This is a self-contained version of some solutions for HoTT-Book's exercises.
The idea is to unpackage all as long as possible to get a better understanding.
Many changes can appear running this experiment. Solutions are
type-checked as a whole using `Agda` `v2.5.3`.

## Requirements

`Agda` has a pragma to be compatible with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="631" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="635" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="643" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="655" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Equality type  also called Identity type can be defined as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="753" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="759" class="Number">4</a> <a id="761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#770" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a>
<a id="765" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="_≡_"></a><a id="770" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#770" class="Datatype Operator">_≡_</a> <a id="774" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="775" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#775" class="Bound">a</a><a id="776" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="778" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="781" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="783" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#775" class="Bound">a</a><a id="788" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="790" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="791" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#791" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="793" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="Bound">A</a><a id="796" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="798" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#779" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="802" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="804" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="808" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#775" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="810" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Chapter 1

### Exercise 1.1

{: .exercise }
  Given functions $f : A \rightarrow B$ and $g : B \to C$, define
  their composite $g\circ f:A\to C$.
  Show that we have $h \circ (g\circ f) \equiv (h\circ g)\circ f$.

We define the composition operation in `Agda` as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘_"></a><a id="2088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2088" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="2092" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2094" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2096" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2097" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="2099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2099" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2101" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2101" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2102" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2104" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2105" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2107" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2109" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2097" class="Bound">i</a><a id="2114" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2116" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2118" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2120" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2099" class="Bound">j</a><a id="2125" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2127" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2127" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2129" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2131" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2101" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2136" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Exercise 1.2

{: .exercise }
  Derive the recursion principle for products $\rec_{A\times B}$
  using only the projections, and verify that the definitional equalities
  are valid. Do the same for $\Sigma$-types.

To solve this problem we need to know:

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    {:.eq}
      $$ \rec_{ A \times B}
        : \prod\limits_{C : \U} (A \to B \to C) → A \times B \to C.
      $$

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $ \rec_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}
      : \prod\limits_{(C : U)} (\Pi_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C) \rightarrow
        \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C
    $
    </p>

<div class="proof" id="proof-1.2">
Proof.<br/>
For products:<br/>
If we have the projections,
$\proj_1 : A \times B \to \mathsf{A}$ and $\proj_2 : A \times B \to \mathsf{B}$,
then $\rec_2$ is another inhabitant where

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
&\rec_1 : \prod\limits_{C : \U} (A \to B \to C) \to A \times B \to C\\
&\rec_1~C~g~c~:\equiv~g~(\proj_1 c,~\proj_2 c).
\end{align*}
$
</p>
By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $\rec_{ A \times B}$ and $\rec_1$.
<br/>
<br/>
For sums:<br/>
The projections are $\proj_1 : \sum_{x : A}  Bx \to \mathsf{A}$ and
$\proj_2 :  \prod {(p : \sum_{x : A}  Bx)} \to \mathsf{B} (\proj_1 p)$.<br/>
By using these projections, we got another recursor defined as follows:
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&\rec_2 : \prod\limits_{C : \U}  (\prod_{x : A} Bx \to C) \to \sum\limits_{x : A} B x \to C\\
&\rec_2~C~g~c~=~g~(\proj_1 c)~(\proj_2 c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $\rec_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}$ and $\rec_2$.
</div>

Now, I'm gonna use the universe levels from Agda in
the following exercises, including this one:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4275" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="4280" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="4287" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a>
  <a id="4304" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="4310" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4311" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#408" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4316" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4318" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">_⊔_</a><a id="4321" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4323" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#611" class="Primitive">lzero</a><a id="4328" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4330" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a><a id="4334" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Σ-type (sigma type) definition (see the definition without projections
[here](https://github.com/jonaprieto/hott-book/blob/master/other/prelim.agda#L20)):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4517" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁"></a><a id="4524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4524" class="Module">Σ-Def₁</a> <a id="4531" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="4607" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ._,_"></a><a id="4619" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4619" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
    <a id="4627" class="Keyword">field</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₁"></a><a id="4639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4639" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="4645" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4556" class="Bound">A</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₂"></a><a id="4655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4655" class="Field">proj₂</a> <a id="4661" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4568" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="4665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4639" class="Field">proj₁</a>

  <a id="4674" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="4679" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="4681" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="4688" class="Comment">-- _,_ : (proj₁ : A) → B proj₁ → Σ A B.</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Its recursor with a function $g : \prod_{(x : A)} B(x)\rightarrow C$
that we provide.

On the other hand, the product type is just a particular case of the sigma type
when the codomain is not dependent, as we can see next by omitting the argument
in `(λ _ → B)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5311" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₁"></a><a id="5318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5318" class="Module">×-Def₁</a> <a id="5325" class="Keyword">where</a>

Its recursor with a function $g : A \rightarrow B \rightarrow C$ that we provide.

### Exercise 1.3

<p class="exercise">
Derive the induction principle for products $\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$,
using only the projections and the propositional uniqueness principle
$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$.
Verify that the definitional equalities are valid.
</p>

To solve this problem, recall the uniqueness principle (Pp. 29. HoTT-Book)

- The **propositional uniqueness principle** says that
every element of $A\times B$ is equal to a pair.

<p class="equation">
  $ \mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}
     : \prod_{(x : A \times B)} ((\proj_{1}(x) , \proj_{2}(x))
       \equiv_{A\times B} x).
  $
</p>

Product type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6454" class="Comment">-- this would be trivial in agda due to definitional η for records</a>
<a id="6521" class="Comment">-- so Capriotti defined a product type without η:</a>

Projections and $\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6908" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Fun₂"></a><a id="6915" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6915" class="Module">×-Fun₂</a> <a id="6922" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6923" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="6925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6925" class="Bound">j</a><a id="6926" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6928" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6932" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6936" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6923" class="Bound">i</a><a id="6937" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6939" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6941" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6943" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6925" class="Bound">j</a><a id="6948" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6950" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="6958" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6578" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="6970" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="6976" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6978" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6599" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="6981" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="6982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6655" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="6985" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="6987" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6678" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="6992" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="6994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6759" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="6999" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="7004" class="Comment">-- propositional uniqueness principle:</a>

  <a id="7453" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7365" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="7459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#818" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#818" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="7469" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7471" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#818" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The induction principle for the product type:

<p class="equation">
$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B} : \prod\limits_{C : A \times B \to \U}
  \left( \prod\limits_{x:A}\ \prod\limits_{y:B}\ \,C( (x,y) ) \right)
  \to \prod\limits_{x:A \times B}\ \,C(x)
$
</p>

        <a id="7914" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7916" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="7918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7918" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7920" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7922" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7774" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7923" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="7925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7925" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="7927" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7785" class="Bound">B</a><a id="7930" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7932" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7887" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="7936" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7918" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6655" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="7941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7925" class="Bound">y</a><a id="7942" class="Symbol">))</a>

<p class="exercise">
Generalize $\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$ to Σ-types, and do the same for
$\Sigma$-types, i.e. show induction and verify that the definitional equality
is valid.
</p>

Σ-type definition using `data`:

Projections and uniqueness propositional principle:

  <a id="8688" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="8693" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8447" class="Module">Σ-Def₂</a> <a id="8700" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="8706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8468" class="Datatype">Σ</a><a id="8708" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="8710" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8526" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a> <a id="8714" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="9313" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9162" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="9319" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9319" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9321" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9321" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9323" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9323" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9325" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9325" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9327" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#818" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Exercise 1.4

<div class="exercise">
Assuming as given only the <em>iterator</em> for natural numbers
<p class="equation">
$\mathsf{ite} : \prod\limits_{C:\U} C \to (C \to C) \to \N \to C $
</p>
with the defining equations
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,0)               &\equiv c_0, \\
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,\mathsf{suc}(n)) &\equiv c_s(\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,n)),
\end{align*}
$
</p>
derive a function having the type of the recursor $\rec$.
Show that the defining equations of the recursor hold propositionally for this
function, using the induction principle for $\N$.
</div>

To solve this problem, let us define the recursor and also the induction principle
for natural numbers. (See more details about these functions in
[Induction on Natural Numbers]({% post_url 2018-02-12-induction-on-natural-numbers %})).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10212" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Def"></a><a id="10219" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10219" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10225" class="Keyword">where</a>

Now, we define the iterator following the equations above:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10732" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Fun"></a><a id="10739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10739" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="10745" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="10753" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10219" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10764" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="10770" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10771" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10239" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="10772" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="10774" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10257" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="10778" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="10780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10270" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="10783" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="10787" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="10792" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10291" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="10798" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="10804" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10805" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10318" class="Function">rec</a><a id="10808" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ℕ-Fun.ite"></a><a id="10813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10813" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10817" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10819" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="10821" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10824" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10826" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="10829" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10831" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10833" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10835" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10837" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10840" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10842" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">C</a><a id="10843" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10845" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10847" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10239" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="10849" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10851" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10822" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="10855" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10813" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10859" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10859" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10861" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10861" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10864" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10864" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10867" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10257" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>    <a id="10875" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10877" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10861" class="Bound">c₀</a>
  <a id="10882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10813" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10886" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10888" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10891" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10891" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10895" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10270" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="10899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10899" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10900" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10902" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10891" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10907" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10908" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10813" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="10912" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10886" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="10914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10888" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="10917" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10891" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="10920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10899" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10921" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Then, we now can define the recursor using this `ite` by iterating over the type
`ℕ × C` (*reloading recursion*?).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11065" class="Comment">-- recursor</a>
  <a id="11079" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6578" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="11091" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11097" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6599" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="11101" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11103" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6678" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="11108" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11110" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6759" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="11115" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6655" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="11120" class="Symbol">)</a>

           <a id="11225" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11226" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10257" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="11231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6655" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="11233" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11185" class="Bound">c₀</a><a id="11235" class="Symbol">)</a>

           <a id="11318" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11191" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11319" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we need to establish the propositional equality between these two
definitions of recursor, i.e, between `rec` and `rec₂`. Let's use
induction to prove that.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11509" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ex1-4"></a><a id="11516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11516" class="Module">ex1-4</a> <a id="11522" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="11565" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10291" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="11576" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11582" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10318" class="Function">rec</a><a id="11586" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11590" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10442" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a> <a id="11601" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11607" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11608" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10469" class="Function">ind</a><a id="11611" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11615" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10739" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="11626" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10813" class="Function">ite</a><a id="11636" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11638" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11125" class="Function">rec₂</a><a id="11642" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="11647" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6578" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="11659" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6599" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="11669" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11671" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6678" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="11676" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11678" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6759" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="11683" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#6655" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="11688" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ex1-4.proof"></a><a id="11707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11707" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="11713" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11715" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11716" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11716" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11718" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11720" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="11723" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="11725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11725" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11728" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11716" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11731" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="11733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11733" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11736" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11738" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10239" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11740" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11742" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11716" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11744" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11716" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11747" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="11757" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11759" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11761" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11762" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link ### Exercise 1.5

{: .exercise}

  Show that if we define $$A+B :\equiv \sum\limits_{(x : \two)} \rec_{\two} (\U, A , B, x),$$
  then we can give a definition of $\ind_{A + B}$ for which the
  definitional equalities holds.

To solve this problem, let me introduce the $\two$ type, which is, the
type only two constructors, the **Booleans**.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12625" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁"></a><a id="12632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12632" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="12639" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12648" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚"></a><a id="12653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12653" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="12655" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12657" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="12661" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟘"></a><a id="12671" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12671" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="12673" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12675" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12653" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟙"></a><a id="12681" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12681" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="12683" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12685" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12653" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


With the recursor:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12733" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Rec₁"></a><a id="12740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12740" class="Module">𝟚-Rec₁</a> <a id="12747" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12756" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12632" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a>  <a id="12769" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12775" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12776" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12671" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="12777" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="12778" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12681" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="12779" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="12780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12653" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="12781" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="13537" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13498" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="13541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13541" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="13543" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13545" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13546" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12681" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13548" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4619" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13541" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13551" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Now, let's try to define the recursor for this coproduct, and later,
we'll try the dependent version of it to complete the exercise.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13713" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Rec₁"></a><a id="13720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13720" class="Module">+-Rec₁</a> <a id="13727" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13736" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13185" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="13748" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13754" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13305" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="13758" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="13760" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13440" class="Function">inl</a><a id="13763" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13498" class="Function">inr</a><a id="13767" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13768" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4619" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="13771" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13775" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13780" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12632" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="13787" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13793" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13794" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12671" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="13795" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12681" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="13797" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12653" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="13799" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="13850" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13852" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13819" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13855" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13857" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13833" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13858" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13866" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13869" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13821" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13871" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13873" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13833" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13874" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13882" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13819" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13305" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="13888" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13821" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13890" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13892" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13833" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="13896" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13804" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13900" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13900" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13902" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13905" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12671" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="13907" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4619" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13909" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13909" class="Bound">a</a><a id="13910" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13912" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13914" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13900" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13916" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13909" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="13920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13804" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="13924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13924" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="13926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13926" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13928" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12681" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13931" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4619" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13933" class="Bound">b</a><a id="13934" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13936" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13938" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13926" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="13940" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13933" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Notice how the recursor of the coproduct matches with the elimination
rule of the disjunction conective also called *case analysis*. That's follows from the
[**propositions-as-types**](https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/propositions+as+types).

![path](/assets/latexit-images/disj-elimination.png){: width="%50" }

Finally, the induction principle for the coproduct:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14330" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Ind₁"></a><a id="14337" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14337" class="Module">+-Ind₁</a> <a id="14344" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14353" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13185" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="14365" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14371" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14372" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13305" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="14375" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13440" class="Function">inl</a><a id="14380" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14381" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13498" class="Function">inr</a><a id="14384" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14386" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4619" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="14389" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14393" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14398" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12632" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="14405" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14412" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12671" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="14413" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14414" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12681" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="14415" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12653" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="14417" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Ind₁.ind"></a><a id="14422" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14422" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="14426" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14428" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14430" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14431" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14431" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14433" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14433" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14434" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14436" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14437" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14439" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14441" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14443" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14447" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14431" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14448" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14450" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14453" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14437" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13305" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14459" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14439" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14461" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14463" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14433" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14468" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="14476" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14478" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14480" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="14482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14437" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14485" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14487" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14491" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14492" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13440" class="Function">inl</a> <a id="14496" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14480" class="Bound">a</a><a id="14497" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="14506" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14508" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14510" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="14512" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14514" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14439" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14515" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14517" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14519" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14521" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13498" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="14526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14510" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14527" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="14536" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14539" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14543" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14437" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13305" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14439" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14548" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14550" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14451" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14554" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14539" class="Bound">p</a>

### Exercise 1.6

<div class="exercise" id="ex-1.6">
Show that if we define $A \times B :≡ \prod_{x:\mathbf{2}}\rec_{\mathbf{2}}\ (\U\, A\, B\, x)$,
then we can give a definition of $\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$ for which the definitional
equalities propositionally (i.e. using equality types).
</div>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15313" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₃"></a><a id="15320" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15320" class="Module">×-Def₃</a> <a id="15327" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="15335" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15340" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12632" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="15347" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="15353" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15354" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12671" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="15355" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12681" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="15357" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12653" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="15359" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15361" class="Keyword">public</a>

### Exercise 1.8

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.8">

Define multiplication and exponentiation using $\rec{\N}$.
Verify that $(\N,+,0,\times,1)$ is a semiring using only
$\ind{\N}$.

</div>


<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>
Operation definitions:

}}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17406" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17410" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10239" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="17411" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17413" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17415" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10239" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="17416" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17418" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="17421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17421" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="17423" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10270" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="17429" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10257" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="17433" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17435" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="17438" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17438" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="17440" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17440" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="17442" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17442" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17444" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17281" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="17452" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17442" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="17454" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17455" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17440" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="17457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17442" class="Bound">m</a><a id="17458" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

On the other hand, a **semiring** is a type? together with two binary operators S(+,*) satisfying the following conditions:

1. Additive associativity: $\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a+b)+c=a+(b+c)$.

2. Additive commutativity: $\prod_{a,b : S}  a+b=b+a$.

3. Multiplicative associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a*b)*c=a*(b*c)$$.

4. Left and right distributivity:

$$\prod_{a,b,c : S} a*(b+c)=(a*b)+(a*c)\text{  and  } \prod_{a,b,c : S} (b+c)*a=(b*a)+(c*a).$$

</div>

### Exercise 1.9

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.9">

Define the type family $\mathsf{Fin} : \N \to \U$ mentioned
at the end of Section 1.3, and the dependent function $\mathsf{fmax} :
\prod_{n:\N} \mathsf{Fin}(n+1)$ mentioned in Section 1.4.
</div>

### Exercise 1.11

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.11">
Show that for any type $A$, we have $\neg\neg\neg A \to \neg A$.
</div>

A propositional logic proof using [Agda-Prop](http://github.com/jonaprieto/agda-prop)
library:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="19350" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-11"></a><a id="19357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19357" class="Module">Ex1-11</a> <a id="19364" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="19372" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="19377" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="19384" href="Data.PropFormula.html" class="Module">Data.PropFormula</a> <a id="19401" class="Number">1</a>

  <a id="Ex1-11.proof"></a><a id="19406" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19406" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="19412" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19414" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19416" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19417" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19417" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19418" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19420" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19421" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19422" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="19432" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19417" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19436" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1657" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="19438" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19440" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19442" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19421" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19446" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#919" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊃</a> <a id="19448" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19450" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19421" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="19454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19406" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="19460" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19461" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19461" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19462" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19465" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19467" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="19473" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#3276" class="InductiveConstructor">⊃-intro</a>
      <a id="19487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19488" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
          <a id="19506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19507" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
              <a id="19528" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19529" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="19536" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19538" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19539" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19546" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19547" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19549" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19551" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19461" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="19552" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19554" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19555" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19558" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19560" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19561" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19563" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19564" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="19584" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19585" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
                <a id="19609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19610" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
                  <a id="19635" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19636" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19643" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19644" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19646" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19461" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19650" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19652" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19654" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19656" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="19660" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19663" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19666" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19669" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="19690" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19691" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="19698" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19699" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19701" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19702" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19704" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19705" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="19712" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19713" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="19715" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19461" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="19719" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="19721" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19723" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19725" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="19727" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19728" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#19464" class="Bound">A</a><a id="19731" class="Symbol">))))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In type theory, the term is:

$$
λ (x : ((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) (a : A) . x ((λ h : A → ⊥) . ha) :
((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) → (A → ⊥)
$$

### Exercise 1.16

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.16">
Show that addition of natural numbers is commutative:
$\prod\limits_{i,j : \N}\ (i + j = j + i).$
</div>

Hint: by induction twice.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20084" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-16"></a><a id="20091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20091" class="Module">Ex1-16</a> <a id="20098" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20106" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20111" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10219" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a>
  <a id="20119" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10442" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a>
  <a id="20132" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20137" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17175" class="Module">Ex1-8</a> <a id="20143" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="20149" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17216" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="20153" class="Symbol">)</a>

                      <a id="20901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20716" class="Bound">hyp₂</a><a id="20905" class="Symbol">)))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Chapter 2

### Exercise 2.6

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.6">
Prove that if $p : x \equiv y$, then the function
$(p \cdot -) : (y \equiv z) \to (x \equiv z)$ is an equivalence.
</div>

![path-triangle](/assets/ipe-images/path-triangle.png){: width="%30" }

<div class="proof">
Solution. <br/>

To show the equivalence, it suffices to show a function
$g : x \equiv z \to y \equiv z$ such that we can prove
$ (p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \id_{x \equiv z}$ and
$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \id_{y \equiv z}$.

Let's define the function $g$.
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
&g : x ≡ z → y ≡ z\\
&g~m~=~\trans~(\sym~p)~m
\end{align*}
$
</p>
<br/>

($(p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \id_{x \equiv z}$):
Let be $m : x ≡ z$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
(p \cdot -) \circ g (m) &= (p \cdot -)~(g~m)\\
                        &= (p \cdot -)~(\trans~(\sym~p)~m)\\
                        &= \trans~p~(\trans~(\sym~p)~m)\\
                        &= \trans~(\trans~p~(\sym~p))~m\\
                        &= \trans~\refl_{x≡z}~m\\
                        &= m
\end{align*}
$
</p>
<br/>
($ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \id_{y \equiv z}$):
Let be $n : y ≡ z$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
g \circ (p \cdot -) n &= g (\trans~p~n)\\
                      &= (\trans~(\sym~p)~(\trans~p~n)\\
                      &= \trans~(\trans~(\sym~p)~p)~n\\
                      &= \trans~\refl_{y ≡ z}~n\\
                      &= n.
\end{align*}
$
</p>

</div>


### Exercise 2.10

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.10">
Prove that ∑-types are associative, in that for any $A : \U$
and families $B : A  \to U$ and $C : \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \to \U$,
we have
<p class="equation">
$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \simeq \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$.
</p>
</div>

<div class="proof" id="proof-2.10">
Solution.<br/>
We can prove that the following functions $f$ and $g$ are inverses.

<p class="equation">
$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \overset{f}{\underset{g}{\rightleftarrows}} \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$.
</p>
defined by $f(a,b,c) :\equiv ((a,b),c)$ and $g(z,c) :\equiv (\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z, c)$.<br/>
Indeed,
<p class="equation">
$
\begin{align*}
(f \circ g) (z, c) &:\equiv f (g (z,c))\\
&:\equiv f\,(\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z, c)\\
&:\equiv ((\proj_1 z,\proj_{2} z), c)
\end{align*}
$
</p>
</div>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.f-g"></a><a id="23689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23689" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="23693" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23695" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23697" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23698" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23698" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23700" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23702" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23705" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23707" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23708" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23708" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23710" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23712" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23698" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23714" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23716" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23719" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23721" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23722" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="23724" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23726" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23698" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23708" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23732" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23734" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23737" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="23747" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23749" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23750" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23750" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23752" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23754" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23756" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23757" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23759" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23698" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23708" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23762" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23764" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23722" class="Bound">C</a><a id="23765" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="23775" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23777" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23388" class="Function">f</a> <a id="23779" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23780" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="23782" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23698" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23785" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23787" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="23789" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23791" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23708" class="Bound">B</a><a id="23792" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="23794" class="Argument">C</a> <a id="23796" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23722" class="Bound">C</a><a id="23799" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23801" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23802" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23529" class="Function">g</a> <a id="23804" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23750" class="Bound">x</a><a id="23805" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23807" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#770" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="23809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23750" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="23813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23689" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="23817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23817" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="23819" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#818" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.g-f"></a><a id="23829" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23829" class="Function">g-f</a> <a id="23833" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23835" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="23837" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23838" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23840" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23842" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23845" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23847" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23848" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23848" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23850" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23852" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23838" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23854" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23856" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23859" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23861" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23862" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="23864" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23866" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4547" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="23868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23838" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23848" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="23872" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23874" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="23877" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="23887" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23890" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#23890" ### Exercise 2.13

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.13">
Show that $(\two \simeq \two) \simeq \two$.
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>

The following text is from [Jdoughertyii](https://github.com/jdoughertyii/hott-exercises/blob/master/Ch02.v).<br/>
The result essentially says that $\two$ is equivalent to itself in two ways:
the identity provides one equivalence, and negation gives the other.  So we
first define these.  $\id_{\two}$ is its own quasi-inverse; we have
$\id_{\two} \circ \id_{\two} \equiv \id_{\two}$, so $\id_{\two}
\circ \id_{\two}
\sim \id_{\two}$ easily.  $\lnot$ is also its own quasi-inverse, since for
any $x$, $\lnot\lnot x = x$.
To show the result, we need to map $\id_{\two}$ and $\lnot$ onto $\two$ is
a quasi-invertible way.  But we need to define this map on all of $\two \simeq \two$.
So for any $h : \two\simeq \two$, let $f(h) = h(\zero_{\two})$, and define
$g : \two \to (\two \simeq \two)$ by

{: .equation}
  $$ g(\zero_{\two}) = \id_{\two}$$ and  $$g(\one_{\two}) = \lnot.$$

To show that these are quasi-inverses,
note first that whatever else is the case, an equivalence
$\two \simeq \two$ can't be a constant function, which we can prove by a case
analysis. Each of $f(\zero_{\two})$ and $f(\one_{\two})$ is in $\two$, so it is
either $\zero_{\two}$ or $\one_{\two}$.

So we have the cases:
 - $f(\zero_{\two}) = f(\one_{\two})$, in which case we can apply $f^{-1}$ to either side to get a contradiction, or
 - $f(\zero_{\two}) = \lnot f(\one_{\two})$. In which case we have the result
Showing that $f \circ g \sim \id_{\two}$ is easy, since we can do it by
cases.  We have

$$\begin{align*}
  f(g(\zero_{\two})) &= f(\id_{\two}) = \id_{\two}(\zero_{\two}) = \zero_{\two}
  \\
  f(g(\one_{\two})) &= f(\lnot) = \lnot \zero_{\two} = \one_{\two}
\end{align*}$$

For the other direction, suppose that $h : \two \simeq \two$ and that
function extensionality holds.
$h(\zero_{\two})$ is either $\zero_{\two}$ or $\one_{\two}$.  If the first, then
because $h$ isn't constant we have $h(\one_{\two}) = \lnot h(\zero_{\two}) =
\one_{\two}$, hence $h = \id_{\two}$.  Furthermore,

$$g(f(h)) = g(h(\zero_{\two})) = g(\zero_{\two}) = \id_\two = h$$

The same argument works for the other case. So $f$ is an equivalence, and
$(\two \simeq \two) \simeq \two$.

</div>

### Exercise 2.14

{: .exercise}

  Suppose we add to type theory [the equality reflection
  rule](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IlfQjWqrK6I) which says that if there is
  an element $p : \id(x,y) $, then in fact $ x :\equiv y$. Prove that
  for any $p : \id(x,x)$ we have $p \equiv \refl_x$.

  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.14.png){: width="%30" }


{: .proof}
  Proof.<br/>
  We first fix the type of $$\refl_x$$ in order to apply effectively
  path induction.<br/>
  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.14b.png)
  Now, $$\refl_x$$ and $$p : x = y$$ in the formulation of path induction
  are well-typed. Therefore, by path induction, we show that
  $$\id(p,\mathsf{refl_{x}})$$. Let be $$x : A$$ and $$C :\equiv
  \prod_{y : A} \prod_{p : x \equiv y }\ p \equiv \refl_{x}$$.
  It sufficies to show and inhabitant of $$C(x, \refl_{x})$$, and this is
  $$\refl_{\refl_x} : \refl_x = \refl_x$$.
  By the equation reflection rule, since we have an inhabitant of $$p \equiv
  \refl_x$$, we conclude these terms are judgemental equal, i.e., $$p \equiv \refl_x$$.

### Exercise 2.17

<div class="exercise">
<ul>
  <li> Show that if $A \simeq A$  and $B \simeq B'$, then $(A\times B) \simeq (A'\times B')$. </li>
  <li> Give two proofs of this fact, one using univalence and one not using it, and show that the two proofs are equal.</li>
  <li> Formulate and prove analogous results for the other type formers: $\Sigma$, $\to$, $\Pi$, and $+$. </li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
  Proof.<br/>
  - Assuming Univalence.
  ![path](/assets/latexit-images/hott-ex2.17.png){: width="%50" }
  - Without Univalence, it is easy to prove
  that the function $h$ defined as follows gives us the
  equivalence that we are looking for.
  $$\begin{align*}
  &h : (A\times B) \to (A'\times B')\\
  &h (a , b) = (f\, a, g\, b).
  \end{align*}$$
  With the inverse:
  $$\begin{align*}
  &h^{-1} : (A'\times B') \to (A\times B)\\
  &h^{-1} (a , b) = (f^{-1}\, a, g^{-1}\, b).
  \end{align*}$$
  To prove these proofs are equal it is suffices to
  show these underlying functions are equal.
</div>

## Chapter 3

To solve the following exercises, let us recall a few things:

- The *set* definition in HoTT:

A type $A$ is a **set** if for all $x, y : A$ and
all $p, q : x \equiv y$, we have $ p \equiv q$. In a proposition
we have

$$\mathsf{isSet}(A) :\equiv \prod\limits_{(x,y : A)}\prod\limits_{(p,q : x \equiv y)} (p \equiv q).$$

- The type for equivalence from $A$ to $B$

$$ (A \simeq B) :\equiv \sum\limits_{f : A \to B} \mathsf{isequiv}(f), $$
where
$$
\mathsf{isequiv(f)} :\equiv
  \left (\sum\limits_{g : B \to A} (f \circ g \sim \id_{B})\right) \times
  \left (\sum\limits_{h : B \to A} (h \circ f \sim \id_{A})\right)
$$

- The homotopy concept:

Let $f , g : \prod\limits_{(x:A)} P(x)$ be two sections of a
type family $P : A \to \U$. A **homotopy** from $f$ to $g$
is a dependent function of type

$$(f \sim g) :\equiv \prod\limits_{x : A} (f(x) \equiv g(x)).$$

### Exercise 3.1

{: .exercise"}
  Prove that if $A\simeq B$ and $A$ is a set, then so is $B$.


<div class="proof" id="proof-3.1" markdown="1" >
Proof.<br/>
Let be $x,y : B$ and $p : x \equiv_{B} y$ and $q : x \equiv_{B} y$.
We need to prove $ p \equiv q$.<br/>
Since $A\simeq B$ then there is a function $f : A \to B$ and some
$g : B \to A$ such that $f \circ g \sim id_{B}$.
Using this function $g$ over the path $p$ we get
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} p : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.

We do the same but this time over the path $q$, that is,
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} q : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
Because of $A$ is a set, we have a new path called
$$m :\mathsf{ap}_{g} p \equiv_{gx \equiv_{A} gy} \mathsf{ap}_{g} q$$. <br/>

Now, an action over this path $m$
using the function $$\mathsf{ap}_{f} : x \equiv_{A} y \to f x \equiv_{B} f y$$
will give us

$$
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m :
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q).
$$


By the lemmas in Chapter 2, we do the following reasoning:

$$
\begin{align*}
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q) &=
  \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} q\\
  &=(\text{transporting by using} f \sim g)\\
  &=\mathsf{ap}_{\id_{B}} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\id_{B}} q\\
  &=p \equiv q.
\end{align*}
$$

Then, we have the inhabitant, $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m : p \equiv q$$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.2

{: .exercise}
  Prove that if $A$ and $B$ are sets, then so is $A+B$.

To solve this exercise, we should take a look of some results from Chapter 2,
Section 2.12.

<div class="proof" id="proof-3.2" markdown="1">
Proof.<br/>

Let be $x, y : A + B$, and paths $p : x \equiv y$, $q : x \equiv
y$. Let's get a path $p \equiv q$.  We proceed by case analysis. If
$x :\equiv \mathsf{inl} a$ and $y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$, for
some $a, b : A$ then $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p : a
\equiv_{A} b$$ and $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q : a \equiv_{A}
b$$.

Since $A$ is a set, there is a path between these last two terms,
this is, $$m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p \equiv
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q$$.  Now, an action over this path
$$m$$ using the $$\mathsf{inl}$$ function give us:
$$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}} m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q)$$.<br/>

By path algebra we have $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
m : p \equiv q$$ since $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv p$$.<br/> Following the
same reasoning, we prove the case $$x :\equiv \mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y
:\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$.  For the latest cases, $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$ and $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, we use the
encode-decode method to derive a proof term for 𝟘 from
$p$ and $q$. Then, we may conclude anything we wish, that is, $p\equiv q$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.4

{: .exercise }
  Show that $A$ is a mere proposition if and only
  if $A\to A$ is contractible.

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Proof. <br/>
- We must to show an inhabitant of the following type:

$$
\mathsf{isProp}(A) \to \sum\limits_{f : A \to A}\, \prod\limits_{g : A \to A } f = g.
$$

This is my proposed term:

$$
t :\equiv λ \mathsf{Aprop} \to (\id_{A}, λ (g : A \to A) \to \mathsf{funext} (\lambda (x : A) \to \mathsf{Aprop}~(\mathsf{id}~x)~(g~x)).
$$

- If $A → A$ is contractible, all functions in this type are equal,
then in particular given $x, y : A$, the constant functions $f(w) \equiv x$
and $g(w) \equiv y$ are equal. Then, $\mathsf{happly} (f =_{A \to A} g, w) : x = y$.
Therefore $$A$$ is a mere proposition.

</div>
